\index{faceforward@{faceforward}!luisa::compute::dsl@{luisa::compute::dsl}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{faceforward()}{faceforward()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespaceluisa_1_1compute_1_1dsl_a929c2b27e7db1944349d0961f05e17a7} 
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{main-override-static_8c_a0240ac851181b84ac374872dc5434ee4}{N}}, typename I, typename NRef$>$ \newline
requires any\+\_\+dsl\+\_\+v$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{main-override-static_8c_a0240ac851181b84ac374872dc5434ee4}{N}}, I, NRef$>$ \&\& is\+\_\+same\+\_\+expr\+\_\+v$<$\mbox{\hyperlink{main-override-static_8c_a0240ac851181b84ac374872dc5434ee4}{N}}, I, NRef, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_aaa532191094c0473e36df45f8fed500e}{float3}}$>$\\
auto luisa\+::compute\+::dsl\+::faceforward (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{main-override-static_8c_a0240ac851181b84ac374872dc5434ee4}{N}} \&\&}]{n}{, }\item[{I \&\&}]{i}{, }\item[{NRef \&\&}]{n\+\_\+ref}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}, {\ttfamily [nodiscard]}, {\ttfamily [noexcept]}}

Return face forward vector. faceforward orients a vector to point away from a surface as defined by its normal. If dot(\+Nref, I) \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} 0 faceforward returns N, otherwise it returns -\/N. \Hypertarget{namespaceluisa_1_1compute_1_1dsl_a4fc6693671e8daabadaae31bad415ecb}\index{luisa::compute::dsl@{luisa::compute::dsl}!floor@{floor}}
